    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app',

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer3627110577667496831">A picturesque mountain town, sparks of romance, a threatening mystery, and a secret society of devious women…<br/><br/>“Wonderful characters, a real mix of women with varied strength and foibles” -Goodreads review 5 stars<br/><br/>“I loved the first book in the Sugar Mountain series so I was really second to read the second installment and get back to investigating with the Sugar Mountain Lad</span>
  <span id="freeText3627110577667496831" style="display:none">A picturesque mountain town, sparks of romance, a threatening mystery, and a secret society of devious women…<br /><br />“Wonderful characters, a real mix of women with varied strength and foibles” -Goodreads review 5 stars<br /><br />“I loved the first book in the Sugar Mountain series so I was really second to read the second installment and get back to investigating with the Sugar Mountain Ladies Historical Society” – Goodreads review 5 stars<br /><br />The cozy community of Sugar Mountain, NC harbors an underground society of women. The society itself is not secret—it’s the actual mission of the group that is concealed.<br /><br />Sugar Mountain is a sleepy town bursting with tourists. If you like quirky shops and original artwork, you’ll want to visit. But the local kindergarten teacher, Sarah has a mystery on her hands. All she did was try to help the fire department and now she’s receiving threatening notes. Of course, she takes the frightening messages to her friends in the Sugar Mountain Ladies Historical Society, but even their investigative skills fall short. How will they be able to find the person intent on holding back the fire department and frightening Sarah? <br /><br />Hugh Brockman, the second in command at the firehouse, is taking extra shifts to cope with the shortage of firefighters. When he visits Sarah’s classroom to talk to her students about fire safety, he gets caught up with the lovely teacher and her cryptic mystery. He’s not happy that someone in town is threatening her with bodily harm, and he intends to find out who it is. <br /><br />With every lead shot down and tensions running high, it’s up to the ladies of the society to go undercover in their own town to flush out the culprit. If they’re not successful, the fire department will continue to be undermanned, leaving Sugar Mountain is in danger and Sarah in peril. <br /><br />Join in the continuing antics of the Sugar Mountain Ladies Historical Society and fall in love along with Hugh and Sarah in this heartfelt and comical romantic mystery.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3627110577667496831" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>

  <span id="freeText10061711716327497668" style="display:none">I have read the first installment of this series, Sugar Mountain, and thoroughly enjoyed it! This addition follows the same secret society working together to solve crimes and mysteries in order to protect their beautiful town but with a new lead. Sarah has a mission to keep her charges safe but faces opposition where she least expects, this leads to death threats and Sarah enlisting the help of her faithful friends to figure out who is behind said threats and to succeed in her quest to improve her towns fire department. Throw in some romance and you get a great, intriguing, paging turning mystery full of humour and grace. </span>

<div id="review_3572006917" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3572006917" />
    <a title="Bluebird" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/117450567-bluebird"><img alt="Bluebird" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595940656p2/117450567.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3572006917?book_show_action=true">Sep 29, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bluebird" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bluebird" href="/user/show/117450567-bluebird">Bluebird</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3572006917" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8495255749650301098">Kirsten Fullmer has created the most perfect and picturesque small town that would be a dream to inhabit. The characters are fantastic and in particular the members of the Sugar Mountain Ladies Historical Society, that equally contrast and compliment each other. A theme I am especially fond of is the strong women that Kirsten depicts in her books. The plot itself was very entertaining; the mystery plays out nicely and smoothly with a brewing romance and plenty of lightheartedness thrown in for g</span>
  <span id="freeText8495255749650301098" style="display:none">Kirsten Fullmer has created the most perfect and picturesque small town that would be a dream to inhabit. The characters are fantastic and in particular the members of the Sugar Mountain Ladies Historical Society, that equally contrast and compliment each other. A theme I am especially fond of is the strong women that Kirsten depicts in her books. The plot itself was very entertaining; the mystery plays out nicely and smoothly with a brewing romance and plenty of lightheartedness thrown in for good measure. I think I could happily read and enjoy all of Kirsten's books, she's fab! </span>

          </span>

<div id="review_3536989758" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3536989758" />
    <a title="Pegboard" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47722544-pegboard"><img alt="Pegboard" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1498516338p2/47722544.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3536989758?book_show_action=true">Sep 14, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pegboard" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pegboard" href="/user/show/47722544-pegboard">Pegboard</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3536989758" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17452186720012810336">Where There’s Smoke by Kirsten Fullmer is a fun read that shows the adventures of the Sugar Mountain Ladies Historical Society. One of their newer members, Sarah, stirs up trouble when she pushes for more firefighters in her growing community. She is a dedicated kindergarten teacher who wishes to keep her students safe. She wonders if she pushed too hard when she receives threatening letters. The ladies historical society come into action, they don’t take kindly with someone messing with one of </span>
  <span id="freeText17452186720012810336" style="display:none">Where There’s Smoke by Kirsten Fullmer is a fun read that shows the adventures of the Sugar Mountain Ladies Historical Society. One of their newer members, Sarah, stirs up trouble when she pushes for more firefighters in her growing community. She is a dedicated kindergarten teacher who wishes to keep her students safe. She wonders if she pushed too hard when she receives threatening letters. The ladies historical society come into action, they don’t take kindly with someone messing with one of their own.<br /> <br />Kirsten Fullmer does not disappoint her readers with Where There’s Smoke. I love watching the Sugar Mountain Ladies Historical Society in action. Their unique personalities, careers, and talents make them a force to be reckoned. The author combines the drama of their lives, suspense of Sarah’s history, and the thrill of hunting down the stalker to make this an amazing read. I am really enjoying this series and can’t wait to read the next one, though I am reading them in reverse order.   </span>

          </span>

For their latest mystery, the ladies are investigating a series of threatening notes send to a school teacher, Sarah after she starts campaigning for an expansion of the fire department. It's not all bad for Sarah as there is a new romance blossoming for her with the handsome fireman Hugh, but will she be able t</span>
  <span id="freeText3468127124796335738" style="display:none">I loved the first book in the Sugar Mountain series so I was really second to read the second installment and get back to investigating with the Sugar Mountain Ladies Historical Society. For their latest mystery, the ladies are investigating a series of threatening notes send to a school teacher, Sarah after she starts campaigning for an expansion of the fire department. It's not all bad for Sarah as there is a new romance blossoming for her with the handsome fireman Hugh, but will she be able to let her fears go?<br /><br />Just like the first Sugar Mountain novel, 'Where There's Smoke' is funny, heartfelt, and full of interesting characters. I can wait for my next meeting with the Historical Society.</span>

<div id="review_3581263705" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3581263705" />
    <a title="Sunshine_45" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/118176174-sunshine-45"><img alt="Sunshine_45" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1601882806p2/118176174.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sunshine_45" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sunshine_45" href="/user/show/118176174-sunshine-45">Sunshine_45</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3581263705" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1088083111413480383">Cozy mysteries are by far my favorite book genre and Kirsten Fullmer knows how to write a great one. This is the second instalment of this series and it's kept the same theme, location and characters while still feeling like a unique book, so you could read them all or just the ones that are most interesting to you (although, I'd highly recommend reading them all). The plot itself is exciting and flows well, with some essential romance too. Just brilliant! </span>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5481703384801173753">This second book in the series has all the good things from the first book plus a rousing good story with a bit of mystery mixed in. One of the ladies from the Historical Society finds herself being stalked. She is a kindergarten teacher, well loved by her students and well liked by the other members of the Historical Society. So well liked that the Society takes it on itself to shadow her to find out who is responsible. There is also a new romantic interest, one that our girl isn't sure she wil</span>
  <span id="freeText5481703384801173753" style="display:none">This second book in the series has all the good things from the first book plus a rousing good story with a bit of mystery mixed in. One of the ladies from the Historical Society finds herself being stalked. She is a kindergarten teacher, well loved by her students and well liked by the other members of the Historical Society. So well liked that the Society takes it on itself to shadow her to find out who is responsible. There is also a new romantic interest, one that our girl isn't sure she will be able to handle. At stake is the one firehouse in the little town and the overworked firefighters who work there. The Historical Society has a well-earned reputation for poor pageants, so it is ironic that this next one is where everything comes to a head. I enjoyed reading this book!</span>
  <a data-text-id="5481703384801173753" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_3659516002" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a title="Sandra Lopez" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sandra Lopez" href="/user/show/1366175-sandra-lopez">Sandra Lopez</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3659516002" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15383616938874104196">When Kindergarten teacher, Sarah, receives a threatening note, the Sugar Mountain Ladies Historical Society are on the case. Could it have anything to do with the shortage of fire fighters in town?<br/><br/>Comprised of women around town that work various jobs, the ladies society acts as an underground espionage group—very top secret and very interesting! Occasionally, you get some babbling at the meetings and sometimes there were a few too many ladies to keep track of.<br/><br/>The narrative is pretty nice and eas</span>
  <span id="freeText15383616938874104196" style="display:none">When Kindergarten teacher, Sarah, receives a threatening note, the Sugar Mountain Ladies Historical Society are on the case. Could it have anything to do with the shortage of fire fighters in town?<br /><br />Comprised of women around town that work various jobs, the ladies society acts as an underground espionage group—very top secret and very interesting! Occasionally, you get some babbling at the meetings and sometimes there were a few too many ladies to keep track of.<br /><br />The narrative is pretty nice and easy-going, but it can be kind of slow at times. All the ladies do is try to gather information from the gossipers in town. Too much time was spent on that rather than trying to figure out who sent the threatening note.<br /><br />A decent read, but it takes a while for the smoke to clear up.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15383616938874104196" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it

              <span id="reviewTextContainer3431213329" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer10317923951216909168">I received an ecopy of this book in exchange for an honest review. Thank you.<br/><br/>I enjoyed the plot of this story as the writing carried me swiftly through the book. I thought the characters were perfectly developed for this story line and found myself caring about each of them. The mystery was strongly written and held my interest until the end, leaving me ready for the next book! <br/>I think this is a great weekend, vacation, beach, road trip, anytime read! <br/><br/></span>

<div id="review_3551181471" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3551181471" />
    <a title="Pat Allen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/53171816-pat-allen"><img alt="Pat Allen" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3551181471?book_show_action=true">Sep 15, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pat Allen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pat Allen" href="/user/show/53171816-pat-allen">Pat Allen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/53506342-where-there-s-smoke">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3551181471" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer896311397427998255"><strong>Fire department</strong><br/><br/>I found this story to be a silly. Some parts had validity, such as the teacher who loved her kindergarten children, and asked someone from the fire department to explain what to do and what not to do if a fire occurred in their home. She, Sarah, was traumatised at five when that happened in her family.<br/>Other parts of the story were just plain silly. The fire chief was devoted to his station, but flipped and started sticking notes under the teacher's car windscreen wiper and threate</span>
  <span id="freeText896311397427998255" style="display:none"><strong>Fire department</strong><br /><br />I found this story to be a silly. Some parts had validity, such as the teacher who loved her kindergarten children, and asked someone from the fire department to explain what to do and what not to do if a fire occurred in their home. She, Sarah, was traumatised at five when that happened in her family.<br />Other parts of the story were just plain silly. The fire chief was devoted to his station, but flipped and started sticking notes under the teacher's car windscreen wiper and threatening her all because of her raising concerns about budget shortages. A group of women disguised themselves and tried to find out who was threatening Sarah. <br />There was no credibility to this, since he had no initial reason to paste different font letters together to make threatening notes. At best this story was a frothy bit of nonsence.</span>
  <a data-text-id="896311397427998255" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('5N2tkT6Gg8r18rvVnDe4pdGXyf7eiWhhFZmrDu7Ar0yOCJ+Pblg/Kjf9CVez21Q2hZXZVpMw+YWniqJfQQRSjw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('dU3GKgrotkRO1WeGb96aOpbfVeVKqK0aYM0o73Gk0K8fmPQ0WjYKpIza1QRAMnapwt1FTQcRPP7S3iG+3mAtbA==')})
  }

Veterans and their families deal with the painful aftermath of combat; one in five Americans has been molested; one in four grew up with alcoholics; one in three couples have engaged in physical violence. Such experiences inevitably leave traces on minds, emotions, and even on biology. Sadly, trauma sufferers frequently pass on their stress to their partners and children. Renowned trauma expert Bessel van der Kolk has spent over three decades working with survivors. In The Body Keeps the Score, he transforms our understanding of traumatic stress, revealing how it literally rearranges the brain’s wiring—specifically areas dedicated to pleasure, engagement, control, and trust. He shows how these areas can be reactivated through innovative treatments including neurofeedback, mindfulness techniques, play, yoga, and other therapies. Based on Dr. van der Kolk’s own research and that of other leading specialists, The Body Keeps the Score offers proven alternatives to drugs and talk therapy—and a way to reclaim lives.<\/span>\n  <a <div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer1057080716907762902">Kirsten is a writer with a love of art and design. She worked in the engineering field, taught college, and consulted free lance. Due to health problems, she retired in 2012 to travel with her husband. They live and work full time in a 40' travel trailer with their little dog Bingo. Besides writing romance novels, she enjoys selling art on Etsy and spoiling their three grandchildren. <br/><br/>As a writer, </span>
  <span id="freeText1057080716907762902" style="display:none">Kirsten is a writer with a love of art and design. She worked in the engineering field, taught college, and consulted free lance. Due to health problems, she retired in 2012 to travel with her husband. They live and work full time in a 40' travel trailer with their little dog Bingo. Besides writing romance novels, she enjoys selling art on Etsy and spoiling their three grandchildren. <br /><br />As a writer, Kirsten's goal is to create strong female characters who face challenging, painful, and sometimes comical situations. She believes that the best way to deal with struggle is through friendship and women helping women. She knows good stories are based on interesting and relatable characters.</span>
